GNSS ZOE M8B Arduino Library 1.0.0
This is a library for the GNSS ZOE M8B Module
u-blox_config_keys.h
Go to the documentation of this file.

15 This library handles configuring and handling the responses
16 from a u-blox GPS module. Works with most modules from u-blox including
17 the Zed-F9P, NEO-M8P-2, NEO-M9N, ZOE-M8Q, SAM-M8Q, and many others.
18
19 https://github.com/sparkfun/SparkFun_Ublox_Arduino_Library

21 Development environment specifics:
22 Arduino IDE 1.8.13

43#ifndef __u_blox_config_keys_h__
44#define __u_blox_config_keys_h__
45
46// The following consts are used to generate KEY values for the advanced protocol functions of VELGET/SET/DEL
47const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_1 = 0x01; // One bit
48const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_8 = 0x02; // One byte
49const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_16 = 0x03; // Two bytes
50const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_32 = 0x04; // Four bytes
51const uint8_t VAL_SIZE_64 = 0x05; // Eight bytes
52
53// These are the Bitfield layers definitions for the UBX-CFG-VALSET message (not to be confused with Bitfield deviceMask
54// in UBX-CFG-CFG)
55const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_RAM = (1 << 0);
56const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_BBR = (1 << 1);
57const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_FLASH = (1 << 2);
58const uint8_t VAL_LAYER_ALL = VAL_LAYER_RAM | VAL_LAYER_BBR | VAL_LAYER_FLASH; // Not valid with getVal()
59
60// Below are various Groups, IDs, and sizes for various settings
61// These can be used to call getVal/setVal/delVal
62//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
63const uint8_t VAL_ID_PROT_UBX = 0x01;
64const uint8_t VAL_ID_PROT_NMEA = 0x02;
65const uint8_t VAL_ID_PROT_RTCM3 = 0x04;
66
67const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_I2C = 0x51;
68const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_I2COUTPROT = 0x72;
69const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART1INPROT = 0x73;
70const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART1OUTPROT = 0x74;
71const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART2INPROT = 0x75;
72const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART2OUTPROT = 0x76;
73const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_USBINPROT = 0x77;
74const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_USBOUTPROT = 0x78;
75
76const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_UART_SIZE = VAL_SIZE_1; // All fields in UART group are currently 1 bit
77const uint8_t VAL_GROUP_I2C_SIZE = VAL_SIZE_8; // All fields in I2C group are currently 1 byte
78
79const uint8_t VAL_ID_I2C_ADDRESS = 0x01;
80
81// Below are the key values for a given configuration setting
82
83// CFG-BDS: BeiDou system configuration
84//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
85const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_BDS_USE_PRN_1_TO_5 = 0x10340014; // Use BeiDou geostationary satellites (PRN 1-5)
86
87// CFG-GEOFENCE: Geofencing configuration
88//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
89const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_CONFLVL = 0x20240011; // Required confidence level for state evaluation
90const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_PIO = 0x10240012; // Use PIO combined fence state output
91const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_PINPOL = 0x20240013; // PIO pin polarity
92const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_PIN = 0x20240014; // PIO pin number
93const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE1 = 0x10240020; // Use frst geofence
94const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE1_LAT = 0x40240021; // Latitude of the first geofence circle center
95const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE1_LON = 0x40240022; // Longitude of the first geofence circle center
96const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE1_RAD = 0x40240023; // Radius of the first geofence circle
97const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE2 = 0x10240030; // Use second geofence
98const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE2_LAT = 0x40240031; // Latitude of the second geofence circle center
99const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE2_LON = 0x40240032; // Longitude of the second geofence circle center
100const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE2_RAD = 0x40240033; // Radius of the second geofence circle
101const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE3 = 0x10240040; // Use third geofence
102const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE3_LAT = 0x40240041; // Latitude of the third geofence circle center
103const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE3_LON = 0x40240042; // Longitude of the third geofence circle center
104const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE3_RAD = 0x40240043; // Radius of the third geofence circle
105const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_USE_FENCE4 = 0x10240050; // Use fourth geofence
106const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE4_LAT = 0x40240051; // Latitude of the fourth geofence circle center
107const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE4_LON = 0x40240052; // Longitude of the fourth geofence circle center
108const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_GEOFENCE_FENCE4_RAD = 0x40240053; // Radius of the fourth geofence circle
109
110// CFG-HW: Hardware configuration
111//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
112const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_VOLTCTRL = 0x10a3002e; // Active antenna voltage control flag
113const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_SHORTDET = 0x10a3002f; // Short antenna detection flag
114const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_SHORTDET_POL = 0x10a30030; // Short antenna detection polarity
115const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_OPENDET = 0x10a30031; // Open antenna detection flag
116const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_OPENDET_POL = 0x10a30032; // Open antenna detection polarity
117const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_PWRDOWN = 0x10a30033; // Power down antenna flag
118const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_PWRDOWN_POL = 0x10a30034; // Power down antenna logic polarity
119const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_CFG_RECOVER = 0x10a30035; // Automatic recovery from short state flag
120const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_SWITCH_PIN = 0x20a30036; // ANT1 PIO number
121const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_SHORT_PIN = 0x20a30037; // ANT0 PIO number
122const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_OPEN_PIN = 0x20a30038; // ANT2 PIO number
123const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_ENGINE = 0x20a30054; // Antenna supervisor engine selection
124const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_SHORT_THR = 0x20a30055; // Antenna supervisor MADC engine short detection threshold
125const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_HW_ANT_SUP_OPEN_THR = 0x20a30056; // Antenna supervisor MADC engine open detection threshold
126
127// CFG-I2C: Configuration of the I2C interface
128//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
129const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2C_ADDRESS = 0x20510001; // I2C slave address of the receiver (7 bits)
130const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2C_EXTENDEDTIMEOUT = 0x10510002; // Flag to disable timeouting the interface after 1.5 s
131const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2C_ENABLED = 0x10510003; // Flag to indicate if the I2C interface should be enabled
132
133// CFG-I2CINPROT: Input protocol configuration of the I2C interface
134//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
135const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_UBX = 0x10710001; // Flag to indicate if UBX should be an input protocol on I2C
136const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_NMEA = 0x10710002; // Flag to indicate if NMEA should be an input protocol on I2C
137const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_RTCM3X = 0x10710004; // Flag to indicate if RTCM3X should be an input protocol on I2C
138const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2CINPROT_SPARTN = 0x10710005; // Flag to indicate if SPARTN should be an input protocol on I2C
139
140// CFG-I2COUTPROT: Output protocol configuration of the I2C interface
141//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
142const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2COUTPROT_UBX = 0x10720001; // Flag to indicate if UBX should be an output protocol on I2C
143const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2COUTPROT_NMEA = 0x10720002; // Flag to indicate if NMEA should be an output protocol on I2C
144const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_I2COUTPROT_RTCM3X =
145 0x10720004; // Flag to indicate if RTCM3X should be an output protocol on I2C
146

148//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
149const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_I2C =
150 0x20920001; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the I2C interface
151const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_UART1 =
152 0x20920002; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the UART1 interface
153const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_UART2 =
154 0x20920003; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the UART2 interface
155const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_USB =
156 0x20920004; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the USB interface
157const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_UBX_SPI =
158 0x20920005; // Information message enable flags for the UBX protocol on the SPI interface
159const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_I2C =
160 0x20920006; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the I2C interface
161const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_UART1 =
162 0x20920007; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the UART1 interface
163const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_UART2 =
164 0x20920008; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the UART2 interface
165const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_USB =
166 0x20920009; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the USB interface
167const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_INFMSG_NMEA_SPI =
168 0x2092000a; // Information message enable flags for the NMEA protocol on the SPI interface

170// CFG-ITFM: Jamming and interference monitor configuration
171//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
172const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_BBTHRESHOLD = 0x20410001; // Broadband jamming detection threshold
173const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_CWTHRESHOLD = 0x20410002; // CW jamming detection threshold
174const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_ENABLE = 0x1041000d; // Enable interference detection
175const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_ANTSETTING = 0x20410010; // Antenna setting
176const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_ITFM_ENABLE_AUX = 0x10410013; // Scan auxiliary bands
177
178// CFG-LOGFILTER: Data logger configuration
179//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
180const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_RECORD_ENA = 0x10de0002; // Recording enabled
181const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_ONCE_PER_WAKE_UP_ENA = 0x10de0003; // Once per wake up
182const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_APPLY_ALL_FILTERS = 0x10de0004; // Apply all filter settings
183const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_MIN_INTERVAL = 0x30de0005; // Minimum time interval between loggedpositions
184const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_TIME_THRS = 0x30de0006; // Time threshold
185const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_SPEED_THRS = 0x30de0007; // Speed threshold
186const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_LOGFILTER_POSITION_THRS = 0x40de0008; // Position threshold
187
188// CFG-MOT: Motion detector configuration
189//-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-
190const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_MOT_GNSSSPEED_THRS =
191 0x20250038; // GNSS speed threshold below which platform is considered as stationary (a.k.a. static hold threshold)
192const uint32_t UBLOX_CFG_MOT_GNSSDIST_THRS =
193 0x3025003b; // Distance above which GNSS-based stationary motion is exit (a.k.a. static hold distance threshold)
194
